HOW TO USE THIS CHECKLIST (FOR A FRESH CHAT)
- Goal: Track which Wowhead WotLK gear planner exports have been imported into Goals/wishlistBuildData.lua.
- Each entry is one build export. Format:
  ✅ TIER[_VARIANT] | export: <paste export JSON>
  ✅ ^ "LABEL" | export: <paste export JSON>   (caret means: reuse previous tier in this spec block)
  ❌ TIER | export: (not available, etc)
- When you import a build, replace the leading "-" with ✅ and keep the export JSON.
- If a build already exists in wishlistBuildData.lua but has no export JSON available, add a line with:
  ✅ TIER | export: PREEXISTING
- Keep the file structured by Class -> Spec (see existing layout).
